ACC-001: Privileged Users adminCount1 Error

Category: Access_Control | Severity: high | Findings: 0 | Duration: 252 ms | Score: 0

Misconfiguration: user accounts with adminCount=1 (protected object flag); review for inappropriate persistence of admin protection.

Remediation: Remove inappropriate adminSDHolder protection; relocate accounts to correct OUs with least-privilege delegation; investigate unexpected adminCount=1 on non-privileged users.

References:

  • https://learn.microsoft.com/windows-server/identity/ad-ds/plan/security-best-practices/appendix-c--protected-accounts-and-groups-in-active-directory

DC-033: DCs with SMB Signing Disabled (SYSVOL GPO) Error

Category: Domain_Controllers | Severity: medium | Findings: 0 | Duration: 0 ms | Score: 0

Scans Group Policy SecEdit templates on SYSVOL for SMB server packet signing. Does not use remote registry; requires read access to \\domain\\SYSVOL like any domain-joined client.

Remediation: Set SMB server signing to required via GPO (or remove weak values); validate with security baseline.

References:

  • https://learn.microsoft.com/windows-server/storage/file-server/smb-security

GPO-ACL-001: SYSVOL Policies insecure ACLs Error

Category: Group_Policy | Severity: high | Findings: 0 | Duration: 0 ms | Score: 0

Misconfiguration: GPO folders under SYSVOL\\Policies where Everyone or Authenticated Users have Modify/Write/FullControl (review and tighten).

Remediation: Remove excessive Modify/Write/FullControl from SYSVOL\\Policies subfolders; grant Domain Admins/Creator Owner and required DC groups only; validate GPO delegation.

References:

  • https://learn.microsoft.com/previous-versions/windows/it-pro/windows-server-2003/cc770880(v=ws.10)
  • Group Policy abuse (MITRE T1484.001)

Error: Could not derive DNS domain from defaultNamingContext.

KRB-001: Kerberoastable User Accounts Error

Category: Kerberos_Security | Severity: high | Findings: 0 | Duration: 4 ms | Score: 0

Misconfiguration: Kerberoastable user accounts (SPN on user); overlaps conceptually with ACC-034 — use for Kerberos category reporting.

Remediation: Remove unnecessary SPNs from user accounts; prefer gMSA for services; enforce strong password policy for remaining SPN owners (same as ACC-034).

References:

  • Kerberoasting (MITRE T1558.003)

Error: LDAP query failed: Exception calling "FindAll" with "0" argument(s): "Unknown error (0x80005000)"

KRB-002: AS-REP Roastable Accounts Error

Category: Kerberos_Security | Severity: critical | Findings: 0 | Duration: 5 ms | Score: 0

Misconfiguration: accounts with Kerberos pre-authentication disabled (AS-REP roastable).

Remediation: Enable Kerberos pre-authentication for affected accounts (or disable accounts that do not require interactive logon). Prefer group-based policies over per-account exceptions.

References:

  • https://learn.microsoft.com/windows/security/threat-protection/auditing/event-4768
  • AS-REP roasting (MITRE ATT&CK)

KRB-009: DES-Only Kerberos Users Error

Category: Kerberos_Security | Severity: high | Findings: 0 | Duration: 11 ms | Score: 0

Weak crypto: accounts allowed DES-only Kerberos (UAC bit); disable DES for the domain and clear per-account use of DES-only.

Remediation: Disable DES for Kerberos at domain level; clear the Use Kerberos DES encryption types only flag on accounts; migrate legacy apps off DES.

USR-001: Accounts Vulnerable to ASRepRoasting Error

Category: Users_Accounts | Severity: critical | Findings: 0 | Duration: 6 ms | Score: 0

AS-REP roasting: Kerberos pre-authentication disabled — offline cracking of account passwords without a TGT. Risk: each object returned is a security-relevant finding until remediated or formally accepted.

Remediation: Enable pre-authentication on accounts; use strong passwords; avoid DONT_REQ_PREAUTH except rare documented exceptions.

References:

  • https://learn.microsoft.com/windows-server/security/kerberos/kerberos-authentication-overview
  • MITRE T1558 (Steal or Forge Kerberos Tickets)

Error: LDAP query failed: Exception calling "FindAll" with "0" argument(s): "Unknown error (0x80005000)"

USR-002: Accounts Vulnerable to Kerberoasting Error

Category: Users_Accounts | Severity: high | Findings: 0 | Duration: 5 ms | Score: 0

Kerberoasting: user accounts with SPNs — ticket hashes can be cracked offline. Risk: each object returned is a security-relevant finding until remediated or formally accepted.

Remediation: Remove user SPNs where possible; use gMSA; enforce strong passwords for SPN owners.

References:

  • https://learn.microsoft.com/windows-server/security/kerberos/kerberos-authentication-overview
  • MITRE T1558 (Steal or Forge Kerberos Tickets)

adminCount=1 (adminSDHolder-protected object) — persistence of elevated ACLs or legacy protected state. Risk: each object returned is a security-relevant finding until remediated or formally accepted.

Remediation: Validate protection is intended; remove inappropriate adminCount; align with tiering model.

USR-006: Accounts with DES Encryption Only Error

Category: Users_Accounts | Severity: high | Findings: 0 | Duration: 5 ms | Score: 0

Weak Kerberos encryption (DES / DES-capable) — tickets are easier to crack. Risk: each object returned is a security-relevant finding until remediated or formally accepted.

USR-030: Accounts with KeyCredentialLink Shadow Credentials Error

Category: Users_Accounts | Severity: high | Findings: 0 | Duration: 6 ms | Score: 0

Remediation: Restrict who can write KeyCredentialLink; audit keys on Tier0; remove unauthorized key credentials.

  • https://learn.microsoft.com/windows-server/identity/ad-ds/plan/security-best-practices/appendix-b--privileged-accounts-and-groups-in-active-directory
